<s> the background statements dramatically expanded to over 200 countries and possessions <\s>
<s> a number of new communications entries added <\s>
<s> 2001 background entries completed for all 267 entities in the factbook <\s>
<s> several new hiv aids entries introduced under the people category <\s>
<s> revision begun on individual country maps to include elevation extremes and a partial geographic grid <\s>
<s> weights and measures appendix deleted <\s>
<s> 2002 new entry on distribution of family income gini index added <\s>
<s> revision of individual country maps continued process still ongoing <\s>
<s> 2003 in the economy category petroleum entries added for oil production consumption exports imports and proved reserves as well as natural gas proved reserves <\s>
<s> 2004 bi-weekly updates launched on the world factbook web site <\s>
<s> additional petroleum entries included for natural gas production consumption exports and imports <\s>
<s> in the transportation category under merchant marine subfields added for foreign-owned vessels and those registered in other countries <\s>
<s> descriptions of the many forms of government mentioned in the factbook incorporated into the definitions and notes <\s>
<s> 2005 in the people category a major infectious diseases field added for countries deemed to pose a higher risk for travelers <\s>
<s> in the economy category entries included for current account balance investment public debt and reserves of foreign exchange and gold <\s>
<s> the transnational issues category expanded to include refugees and internally displaced persons <\s>
<s> category headings receive distinctive colored backgrounds <\s>
<s> these distinguishing colors are used in both the printed and online versions of the factbook <\s>
<s> size of the printed factbook reaches 702 pages <\s>
<s> 2006 in the economy category national gdp figures now presented at official exchange rates oer in addition to gdp at purchasing power parity ppp <\s>
<s> entries in the transportation section reordered highways changed to roadways and ports and harbors to ports and terminals <\s>
<s> 2007 in the government category the capital entry significantly expanded with up to four subfields including new information having to do with time <\s>
<s> the subfields consist of the name of the capital itself its geographic coordinates the time difference at the capital from coordinated universal time utc and if applicable information on daylight saving time dst <\s>
<s> where appropriate a special note is added to highlight those countries with multiple time zones <\s>
<s> a trafficking in persons entry added to the transnational issues category <\s>
<s> a new appendix weights and measures re introduced to the online version of the factbook <\s>
<s> 2008 in the geography category two fields focus on the increasingly vital resource of water total renewable water resources and freshwater withdrawal <\s>
<s> in the economy category three fields added for stock of direct foreign investment at home stock of direct foreign investment abroad and market value of publicly traded shares <\s>
<s> concise descriptions of all major religions included in the definitions and notes <\s>
<s> responsibility for printing of the world factbook turned over to the government printing office <\s>
<s> 2009 the online factbook site completely redesigned with many new features <\s>
<s> in the people category two new fields provide information on education in terms of opportunity and resources school life expectancy and education expenditures <\s>
<s> additionally the urbanization entry expanded to include all countries <\s>
<s> in the economy category five fields added central bank discount rate commercial bank prime lending rate stock of money stock of quasi money and stock of domestic credit <\s>
<s> 2010 in order to facilitate comparisons over time dozens of the entries in the economy category expanded to include two and in some cases three years worth of data <\s>
<s> a variety of enhancements introduced on the factbook web site <\s>
<s> 2011 weekly updates inaugurated on the the world factbook web site <\s>
<s> the dissolution of the netherlands antilles results in two new listings curacao and sint maarten <\s>
<s> a broadcast media field replaces the former radio broadcast stations and tv broadcast stations entries <\s>
<s> concise descriptions of all major legal systems incorporated into the definitions and notes <\s>
<s> in the geography section under natural hazards a volcanism subfield added for countries with historically active volcanoes <\s>
<s> in the government category a new national anthems field introduced <\s>
<s> about :: copyright and contributors the world factbook is prepared by the central intelligence agency for the use of us government officials and the style format coverage and content are designed to meet their specific requirements <\s>
<s> information is provided by antarctic information program national science foundation armed forces medical intelligence center department of defense bureau of the census department of commerce bureau of labor statistics department of labor central intelligence agency council of managers of national antarctic programs defense intelligence agency department of defense department of energy department of state fish and wildlife service department of the interior maritime administration department of transportation national geospatial-intelligence agency department of defense naval facilities engineering command department of defense office of insular affairs department of the interior office of naval intelligence department of defense us board on geographic names department of the interior us transportation command department of defense oil gas journal and other public and private sources <\s>
<s> the factbook is in the public domain <\s>
<s> accordingly it may be copied freely without permission of the central intelligence agency cia <\s>
<s> the official seal of the cia however may not be copied without permission as required by the cia act of 1949 50 u s c <\s>
<s> misuse of the official seal of the cia could result in civil and criminal penalties <\s>
<s> 1981 publication becomes an annual product and is renamed the world factbook <\s>
<s> a total of 165 nations are covered on 225 pages <\s>
<s> 1983 appendices conversion factors international organizations first introduced <\s>
<s> 1984 appendices expanded now include a <\s>
<s> the united nations b <\s>
<s> selected united nations organizations c <\s>
<s> selected international organizations d <\s>
<s> country membership in selected organizations e <\s>
<s> 1987 a new geography section replaces the former separate land and water sections <\s>
<s> un organizations and selected international organizations appendices merged into a new international organizations appendix <\s>
<s> 1988 more than 40 new geographic entities added to provide complete world coverage without overlap or omission <\s>
<s> among the new entities are antarctica oceans arctic atlantic indian pacific and the world <\s>
<s> the front-of-the-book explanatory introduction expanded and retitled to notes definitions and abbreviations <\s>
<s> two new appendices added weights and measures in place of conversion factors and a cross-reference list of geographic names <\s>
<s> factbook size reaches 300 pages <\s>
<s> 1989 economy section completely revised and now includes an overview briefly describing a country's economy <\s>
<s> new entries added under people government and communications <\s>
<s> 1990 the government section revised and considerably expanded with new entries <\s>
<s> 1991 a new international organizations and groups appendix added <\s>
<s> factbook size reaches 405 pages <\s>
<s> 1992 twenty new successor state entries replace those of the soviet union and yugoslavia <\s>
<s> new countries are respectively armenia azerbaijan belarus estonia georgia kazakhstan kyrgyzstan latvia lithuania moldova russia tajikistan turkmenistan ukraine uzbekistan and bosnia and hercegovina croatia macedonia serbia and montenegro slovenia <\s>
<s> number of nations in the factbook rises to 188 <\s>
<s> 1993 czechoslovakia's split necessitates new czech republic and slovakia entries <\s>
<s> new eritrea entry added after it secedes from ethiopia <\s>
<s> substantial enhancements made to geography section <\s>
<s> 1994 two new appendices address selected international environmental agreements <\s>
<s> the gross domestic product gdp of most developing countries changed to a purchasing power parity ppp basis rather than an exchange rate basis <\s>
<s> factbook size up to 512 pages <\s>
<s> 1995 the gdp of all countries now presented on a ppp basis <\s>
<s> new appendix lists estimates of gdp on an exchange rate basis <\s>
<s> communications category split railroads highways inland waterways pipelines merchant marine and airports entries now make up a new transportation category <\s>
<s> the world factbook is first produced on cd-rom <\s>
<s> 1996 maps accompanying each entry now present more detail <\s>
<s> flags also introduced for nearly all entities <\s>
<s> various new entries appear under geography and communications <\s>
<s> factbook abbreviations consolidated into a new appendix a <\s>
<s> two new appendices present a cross-reference list of country data codes and a cross-reference list of hydrogeographic data codes <\s>
<s> geographic coordinates added to appendix h cross-reference list of geographic names <\s>
<s> factbook size expands by 95 pages in one year to reach 652 <\s>
<s> 1997 the world factbook introduced onto the internet <\s>
<s> a special printed edition prepared for the cia's 50th anniversary <\s>
<s> a schema or guide to country profiles introduced <\s>
<s> new color maps and flags now accompany each country profile <\s>
<s> category headings distinguished by shaded backgrounds <\s>
<s> number of categories expanded to nine the current number with the addition of an introduction for only a few countries and transnational issues which includes disputes-international and illicit drugs <\s>
<s> 1998 the introduction category with two entries current issues and historical perspective expanded to more countries <\s>
<s> last year for the production of cd-rom versions of the factbook <\s>
<s> 1999 historical perspective and current issues entries in the introduction category combined into a new background statement <\s>

<s> the subfields consist of the name of the capital itself its geographic coordinates the time difference at the capital from coordinated universal time utc and if applicable information on daylight saving time dst <\s>
<s> where appropriate a special note is added to highlight those countries with multiple time zones <\s>
<s> a trafficking in persons entry added to the transnational issues category <\s>
<s> a new appendix weights and measures re introduced to the online version of the factbook <\s>
<s> 2008 in the geography category two fields focus on the increasingly vital resource of water total renewable water resources and freshwater withdrawal <\s>
<s> in the economy category three fields added for stock of direct foreign investment at home stock of direct foreign investment abroad and market value of publicly traded shares <\s>
<s> concise descriptions of all major religions included in the definitions and notes <\s>
<s> responsibility for printing of the world factbook turned over to the government printing office <\s>
<s> 2009 the online factbook site completely redesigned with many new features <\s>
<s> in the people category two new fields provide information on education in terms of opportunity and resources school life expectancy and education expenditures <\s>
<s> additionally the urbanization entry expanded to include all countries <\s>
<s> in the economy category five fields added central bank discount rate commercial bank prime lending rate stock of money stock of quasi money and stock of domestic credit <\s>
<s> 2010 in order to facilitate comparisons over time dozens of the entries in the economy category expanded to include two and in some cases three years worth of data <\s>
<s> a variety of enhancements introduced on the factbook web site <\s>
<s> 2011 weekly updates inaugurated on the the world factbook web site <\s>
<s> the dissolution of the netherlands antilles results in two new listings curacao and sint maarten <\s>
<s> a broadcast media field replaces the former radio broadcast stations and tv broadcast stations entries <\s>
<s> concise descriptions of all major legal systems incorporated into the definitions and notes <\s>
<s> in the geography section under natural hazards a volcanism subfield added for countries with historically active volcanoes <\s>
<s> in the government category a new national anthems field introduced <\s>
<s> about :: copyright and contributors the world factbook is prepared by the central intelligence agency for the use of us government officials and the style format coverage and content are designed to meet their specific requirements <\s>
<s> information is provided by antarctic information program national science foundation armed forces medical intelligence center department of defense bureau of the census department of commerce bureau of labor statistics department of labor central intelligence agency council of managers of national antarctic programs defense intelligence agency department of defense department of energy department of state fish and wildlife service department of the interior maritime administration department of transportation national geospatial-intelligence agency department of defense naval facilities engineering command department of defense office of insular affairs department of the interior office of naval intelligence department of defense us board on geographic names department of the interior us transportation command department of defense oil gas journal and other public and private sources <\s>
<s> the factbook is in the public domain <\s>
<s> accordingly it may be copied freely without permission of the central intelligence agency cia <\s>
<s> the official seal of the cia however may not be copied without permission as required by the cia act of 1949 50 u s c <\s>
<s> misuse of the official seal of the cia could result in civil and criminal penalties <\s>
<s> 1981 publication becomes an annual product and is renamed the world factbook <\s>
<s> a total of 165 nations are covered on 225 pages <\s>
<s> 1983 appendices conversion factors international organizations first introduced <\s>
<s> 1984 appendices expanded now include a <\s>
<s> the united nations b <\s>
<s> selected united nations organizations c <\s>
<s> selected international organizations d <\s>
<s> country membership in selected organizations e <\s>
<s> 1987 a new geography section replaces the former separate land and water sections <\s>
<s> un organizations and selected international organizations appendices merged into a new international organizations appendix <\s>
<s> 1988 more than 40 new geographic entities added to provide complete world coverage without overlap or omission <\s>
<s> among the new entities are antarctica oceans arctic atlantic indian pacific and the world <\s>
<s> the front-of-the-book explanatory introduction expanded and retitled to notes definitions and abbreviations <\s>
<s> two new appendices added weights and measures in place of conversion factors and a cross-reference list of geographic names <\s>
<s> factbook size reaches 300 pages <\s>
<s> 1989 economy section completely revised and now includes an overview briefly describing a country's economy <\s>
<s> new entries added under people government and communications <\s>
<s> 1990 the government section revised and considerably expanded with new entries <\s>
<s> 1991 a new international organizations and groups appendix added <\s>
<s> factbook size reaches 405 pages <\s>
<s> 1992 twenty new successor state entries replace those of the soviet union and yugoslavia <\s>
<s> new countries are respectively armenia azerbaijan belarus estonia georgia kazakhstan kyrgyzstan latvia lithuania moldova russia tajikistan turkmenistan ukraine uzbekistan and bosnia and hercegovina croatia macedonia serbia and montenegro slovenia <\s>
<s> number of nations in the factbook rises to 188 <\s>
<s> 1993 czechoslovakia's split necessitates new czech republic and slovakia entries <\s>
<s> new eritrea entry added after it secedes from ethiopia <\s>
<s> substantial enhancements made to geography section <\s>
<s> 1994 two new appendices address selected international environmental agreements <\s>
<s> the gross domestic product gdp of most developing countries changed to a purchasing power parity ppp basis rather than an exchange rate basis <\s>
<s> factbook size up to 512 pages <\s>
<s> 1995 the gdp of all countries now presented on a ppp basis <\s>
<s> new appendix lists estimates of gdp on an exchange rate basis <\s>
<s> communications category split railroads highways inland waterways pipelines merchant marine and airports entries now make up a new transportation category <\s>
<s> the world factbook is first produced on cd-rom <\s>
<s> 1996 maps accompanying each entry now present more detail <\s>
<s> flags also introduced for nearly all entities <\s>
<s> various new entries appear under geography and communications <\s>
<s> factbook abbreviations consolidated into a new appendix a <\s>
<s> two new appendices present a cross-reference list of country data codes and a cross-reference list of hydrogeographic data codes <\s>
<s> geographic coordinates added to appendix h cross-reference list of geographic names <\s>
<s> factbook size expands by 95 pages in one year to reach 652 <\s>
<s> 1997 the world factbook introduced onto the internet <\s>
<s> a special printed edition prepared for the cia's 50th anniversary <\s>
<s> a schema or guide to country profiles introduced <\s>
<s> new color maps and flags now accompany each country profile <\s>
<s> category headings distinguished by shaded backgrounds <\s>
<s> number of categories expanded to nine the current number with the addition of an introduction for only a few countries and transnational issues which includes disputes-international and illicit drugs <\s>
<s> 1998 the introduction category with two entries current issues and historical perspective expanded to more countries <\s>
<s> last year for the production of cd-rom versions of the factbook <\s>
<s> 1999 historical perspective and current issues entries in the introduction category combined into a new background statement <\s>
<s> several new economy entries introduced <\s>
<s> a new physical map of the world added to the back-of-the-book reference maps <\s>
<s> 2000 a new country profile added on the southern ocean <\s>
<s> the background statements dramatically expanded to over 200 countries and possessions <\s>
<s> a number of new communications entries added <\s>
<s> 2001 background entries completed for all 267 entities in the factbook <\s>
<s> several new hiv aids entries introduced under the people category <\s>
<s> revision begun on individual country maps to include elevation extremes and a partial geographic grid <\s>
<s> weights and measures appendix deleted <\s>
<s> 2002 new entry on distribution of family income gini index added <\s>
<s> revision of individual country maps continued process still ongoing <\s>
<s> 2003 in the economy category petroleum entries added for oil production consumption exports imports and proved reserves as well as natural gas proved reserves <\s>
<s> 2004 bi-weekly updates launched on the world factbook web site <\s>
<s> additional petroleum entries included for natural gas production consumption exports and imports <\s>
<s> in the transportation category under merchant marine subfields added for foreign-owned vessels and those registered in other countries <\s>
<s> descriptions of the many forms of government mentioned in the factbook incorporated into the definitions and notes <\s>
<s> 2005 in the people category a major infectious diseases field added for countries deemed to pose a higher risk for travelers <\s>
<s> in the economy category entries included for current account balance investment public debt and reserves of foreign exchange and gold <\s>
<s> the transnational issues category expanded to include refugees and internally displaced persons <\s>
<s> category headings receive distinctive colored backgrounds <\s>
<s> these distinguishing colors are used in both the printed and online versions of the factbook <\s>
<s> size of the printed factbook reaches 702 pages <\s>
<s> 2006 in the economy category national gdp figures now presented at official exchange rates oer in addition to gdp at purchasing power parity ppp <\s>

<s> in the geography section under natural hazards a volcanism subfield added for countries with historically active volcanoes <\s>
<s> in the government category a new national anthems field introduced <\s>
<s> about :: copyright and contributors the world factbook is prepared by the central intelligence agency for the use of us government officials and the style format coverage and content are designed to meet their specific requirements <\s>
<s> information is provided by antarctic information program national science foundation armed forces medical intelligence center department of defense bureau of the census department of commerce bureau of labor statistics department of labor central intelligence agency council of managers of national antarctic programs defense intelligence agency department of defense department of energy department of state fish and wildlife service department of the interior maritime administration department of transportation national geospatial-intelligence agency department of defense naval facilities engineering command department of defense office of insular affairs department of the interior office of naval intelligence department of defense us board on geographic names department of the interior us transportation command department of defense oil gas journal and other public and private sources <\s>
<s> the factbook is in the public domain <\s>
<s> accordingly it may be copied freely without permission of the central intelligence agency cia <\s>
<s> the official seal of the cia however may not be copied without permission as required by the cia act of 1949 50 u s c <\s>
<s> misuse of the official seal of the cia could result in civil and criminal penalties <\s>
<s> 1981 publication becomes an annual product and is renamed the world factbook <\s>
<s> a total of 165 nations are covered on 225 pages <\s>
<s> 1983 appendices conversion factors international organizations first introduced <\s>
<s> 1984 appendices expanded now include a <\s>
<s> the united nations b <\s>
<s> selected united nations organizations c <\s>
<s> selected international organizations d <\s>
<s> country membership in selected organizations e <\s>
<s> 1987 a new geography section replaces the former separate land and water sections <\s>
<s> un organizations and selected international organizations appendices merged into a new international organizations appendix <\s>
<s> 1988 more than 40 new geographic entities added to provide complete world coverage without overlap or omission <\s>
<s> among the new entities are antarctica oceans arctic atlantic indian pacific and the world <\s>
<s> the front-of-the-book explanatory introduction expanded and retitled to notes definitions and abbreviations <\s>
<s> two new appendices added weights and measures in place of conversion factors and a cross-reference list of geographic names <\s>
<s> factbook size reaches 300 pages <\s>
<s> 1989 economy section completely revised and now includes an overview briefly describing a country's economy <\s>
<s> new entries added under people government and communications <\s>
<s> 1990 the government section revised and considerably expanded with new entries <\s>
<s> 1991 a new international organizations and groups appendix added <\s>
<s> factbook size reaches 405 pages <\s>
<s> 1992 twenty new successor state entries replace those of the soviet union and yugoslavia <\s>
<s> new countries are respectively armenia azerbaijan belarus estonia georgia kazakhstan kyrgyzstan latvia lithuania moldova russia tajikistan turkmenistan ukraine uzbekistan and bosnia and hercegovina croatia macedonia serbia and montenegro slovenia <\s>
<s> number of nations in the factbook rises to 188 <\s>
<s> 1993 czechoslovakia's split necessitates new czech republic and slovakia entries <\s>
<s> new eritrea entry added after it secedes from ethiopia <\s>
<s> substantial enhancements made to geography section <\s>
<s> 1994 two new appendices address selected international environmental agreements <\s>
<s> the gross domestic product gdp of most developing countries changed to a purchasing power parity ppp basis rather than an exchange rate basis <\s>
<s> factbook size up to 512 pages <\s>
<s> 1995 the gdp of all countries now presented on a ppp basis <\s>
<s> new appendix lists estimates of gdp on an exchange rate basis <\s>
<s> communications category split railroads highways inland waterways pipelines merchant marine and airports entries now make up a new transportation category <\s>
<s> the world factbook is first produced on cd-rom <\s>
<s> 1996 maps accompanying each entry now present more detail <\s>
<s> flags also introduced for nearly all entities <\s>
<s> various new entries appear under geography and communications <\s>
<s> factbook abbreviations consolidated into a new appendix a <\s>
<s> two new appendices present a cross-reference list of country data codes and a cross-reference list of hydrogeographic data codes <\s>
<s> geographic coordinates added to appendix h cross-reference list of geographic names <\s>
<s> factbook size expands by 95 pages in one year to reach 652 <\s>
<s> 1997 the world factbook introduced onto the internet <\s>
<s> a special printed edition prepared for the cia's 50th anniversary <\s>
<s> a schema or guide to country profiles introduced <\s>
<s> new color maps and flags now accompany each country profile <\s>
<s> category headings distinguished by shaded backgrounds <\s>
<s> number of categories expanded to nine the current number with the addition of an introduction for only a few countries and transnational issues which includes disputes-international and illicit drugs <\s>
<s> 1998 the introduction category with two entries current issues and historical perspective expanded to more countries <\s>
<s> last year for the production of cd-rom versions of the factbook <\s>
<s> 1999 historical perspective and current issues entries in the introduction category combined into a new background statement <\s>
<s> several new economy entries introduced <\s>
<s> a new physical map of the world added to the back-of-the-book reference maps <\s>
<s> 2000 a new country profile added on the southern ocean <\s>
<s> the background statements dramatically expanded to over 200 countries and possessions <\s>
<s> a number of new communications entries added <\s>
<s> 2001 background entries completed for all 267 entities in the factbook <\s>
<s> several new hiv aids entries introduced under the people category <\s>
<s> revision begun on individual country maps to include elevation extremes and a partial geographic grid <\s>
<s> weights and measures appendix deleted <\s>
<s> 2002 new entry on distribution of family income gini index added <\s>
<s> revision of individual country maps continued process still ongoing <\s>
<s> 2003 in the economy category petroleum entries added for oil production consumption exports imports and proved reserves as well as natural gas proved reserves <\s>
<s> 2004 bi-weekly updates launched on the world factbook web site <\s>
<s> additional petroleum entries included for natural gas production consumption exports and imports <\s>
<s> in the transportation category under merchant marine subfields added for foreign-owned vessels and those registered in other countries <\s>
<s> descriptions of the many forms of government mentioned in the factbook incorporated into the definitions and notes <\s>
<s> 2005 in the people category a major infectious diseases field added for countries deemed to pose a higher risk for travelers <\s>
<s> in the economy category entries included for current account balance investment public debt and reserves of foreign exchange and gold <\s>
<s> the transnational issues category expanded to include refugees and internally displaced persons <\s>
<s> category headings receive distinctive colored backgrounds <\s>
<s> these distinguishing colors are used in both the printed and online versions of the factbook <\s>
<s> size of the printed factbook reaches 702 pages <\s>
<s> 2006 in the economy category national gdp figures now presented at official exchange rates oer in addition to gdp at purchasing power parity ppp <\s>
<s> entries in the transportation section reordered highways changed to roadways and ports and harbors to ports and terminals <\s>
<s> 2007 in the government category the capital entry significantly expanded with up to four subfields including new information having to do with time <\s>
<s> the subfields consist of the name of the capital itself its geographic coordinates the time difference at the capital from coordinated universal time utc and if applicable information on daylight saving time dst <\s>
<s> where appropriate a special note is added to highlight those countries with multiple time zones <\s>
<s> a trafficking in persons entry added to the transnational issues category <\s>
<s> a new appendix weights and measures re introduced to the online version of the factbook <\s>
<s> 2008 in the geography category two fields focus on the increasingly vital resource of water total renewable water resources and freshwater withdrawal <\s>
<s> in the economy category three fields added for stock of direct foreign investment at home stock of direct foreign investment abroad and market value of publicly traded shares <\s>
<s> concise descriptions of all major religions included in the definitions and notes <\s>
<s> responsibility for printing of the world factbook turned over to the government printing office <\s>
<s> 2009 the online factbook site completely redesigned with many new features <\s>
<s> in the people category two new fields provide information on education in terms of opportunity and resources school life expectancy and education expenditures <\s>
<s> additionally the urbanization entry expanded to include all countries <\s>
<s> in the economy category five fields added central bank discount rate commercial bank prime lending rate stock of money stock of quasi money and stock of domestic credit <\s>
<s> 2010 in order to facilitate comparisons over time dozens of the entries in the economy category expanded to include two and in some cases three years worth of data <\s>
<s> a variety of enhancements introduced on the factbook web site <\s>
<s> 2011 weekly updates inaugurated on the the world factbook web site <\s>
<s> the dissolution of the netherlands antilles results in two new listings curacao and sint maarten <\s>
<s> a broadcast media field replaces the former radio broadcast stations and tv broadcast stations entries <\s>
<s> concise descriptions of all major legal systems incorporated into the definitions and notes <\s>
<s> in the geography section under natural hazards a volcanism subfield added for countries with historically active volcanoes <\s>
<s> in the government category a new national anthems field introduced <\s>

<s> 1988 more than 40 new geographic entities added to provide complete world coverage without overlap or omission <\s>
<s> among the new entities are antarctica oceans arctic atlantic indian pacific and the world <\s>
<s> the front-of-the-book explanatory introduction expanded and retitled to notes definitions and abbreviations <\s>
<s> two new appendices added weights and measures in place of conversion factors and a cross-reference list of geographic names <\s>
<s> factbook size reaches 300 pages <\s>
<s> 1989 economy section completely revised and now includes an overview briefly describing a country's economy <\s>
<s> new entries added under people government and communications <\s>
<s> 1990 the government section revised and considerably expanded with new entries <\s>
<s> 1991 a new international organizations and groups appendix added <\s>
<s> factbook size reaches 405 pages <\s>
<s> 1992 twenty new successor state entries replace those of the soviet union and yugoslavia <\s>
<s> new countries are respectively armenia azerbaijan belarus estonia georgia kazakhstan kyrgyzstan latvia lithuania moldova russia tajikistan turkmenistan ukraine uzbekistan and bosnia and hercegovina croatia macedonia serbia and montenegro slovenia <\s>
<s> number of nations in the factbook rises to 188 <\s>
<s> 1993 czechoslovakia's split necessitates new czech republic and slovakia entries <\s>
<s> new eritrea entry added after it secedes from ethiopia <\s>
<s> substantial enhancements made to geography section <\s>
<s> 1994 two new appendices address selected international environmental agreements <\s>
<s> the gross domestic product gdp of most developing countries changed to a purchasing power parity ppp basis rather than an exchange rate basis <\s>
<s> factbook size up to 512 pages <\s>
<s> 1995 the gdp of all countries now presented on a ppp basis <\s>
<s> new appendix lists estimates of gdp on an exchange rate basis <\s>
<s> communications category split railroads highways inland waterways pipelines merchant marine and airports entries now make up a new transportation category <\s>
<s> the world factbook is first produced on cd-rom <\s>
<s> 1996 maps accompanying each entry now present more detail <\s>
<s> flags also introduced for nearly all entities <\s>
<s> various new entries appear under geography and communications <\s>
<s> factbook abbreviations consolidated into a new appendix a <\s>
<s> two new appendices present a cross-reference list of country data codes and a cross-reference list of hydrogeographic data codes <\s>
<s> geographic coordinates added to appendix h cross-reference list of geographic names <\s>
<s> factbook size expands by 95 pages in one year to reach 652 <\s>
<s> 1997 the world factbook introduced onto the internet <\s>
<s> a special printed edition prepared for the cia's 50th anniversary <\s>
<s> a schema or guide to country profiles introduced <\s>
<s> new color maps and flags now accompany each country profile <\s>
<s> category headings distinguished by shaded backgrounds <\s>
<s> number of categories expanded to nine the current number with the addition of an introduction for only a few countries and transnational issues which includes disputes-international and illicit drugs <\s>
<s> 1998 the introduction category with two entries current issues and historical perspective expanded to more countries <\s>
<s> last year for the production of cd-rom versions of the factbook <\s>
<s> 1999 historical perspective and current issues entries in the introduction category combined into a new background statement <\s>
<s> several new economy entries introduced <\s>
<s> a new physical map of the world added to the back-of-the-book reference maps <\s>
<s> 2000 a new country profile added on the southern ocean <\s>
<s> the background statements dramatically expanded to over 200 countries and possessions <\s>
<s> a number of new communications entries added <\s>
<s> 2001 background entries completed for all 267 entities in the factbook <\s>
<s> several new hiv aids entries introduced under the people category <\s>
<s> revision begun on individual country maps to include elevation extremes and a partial geographic grid <\s>
<s> weights and measures appendix deleted <\s>
<s> 2002 new entry on distribution of family income gini index added <\s>
<s> revision of individual country maps continued process still ongoing <\s>
<s> 2003 in the economy category petroleum entries added for oil production consumption exports imports and proved reserves as well as natural gas proved reserves <\s>
<s> 2004 bi-weekly updates launched on the world factbook web site <\s>
<s> additional petroleum entries included for natural gas production consumption exports and imports <\s>
<s> in the transportation category under merchant marine subfields added for foreign-owned vessels and those registered in other countries <\s>
<s> descriptions of the many forms of government mentioned in the factbook incorporated into the definitions and notes <\s>
<s> 2005 in the people category a major infectious diseases field added for countries deemed to pose a higher risk for travelers <\s>
<s> in the economy category entries included for current account balance investment public debt and reserves of foreign exchange and gold <\s>
<s> the transnational issues category expanded to include refugees and internally displaced persons <\s>
<s> category headings receive distinctive colored backgrounds <\s>
<s> these distinguishing colors are used in both the printed and online versions of the factbook <\s>
<s> size of the printed factbook reaches 702 pages <\s>
<s> 2006 in the economy category national gdp figures now presented at official exchange rates oer in addition to gdp at purchasing power parity ppp <\s>
<s> entries in the transportation section reordered highways changed to roadways and ports and harbors to ports and terminals <\s>
<s> 2007 in the government category the capital entry significantly expanded with up to four subfields including new information having to do with time <\s>
<s> the subfields consist of the name of the capital itself its geographic coordinates the time difference at the capital from coordinated universal time utc and if applicable information on daylight saving time dst <\s>
<s> where appropriate a special note is added to highlight those countries with multiple time zones <\s>
<s> a trafficking in persons entry added to the transnational issues category <\s>
<s> a new appendix weights and measures re introduced to the online version of the factbook <\s>
<s> 2008 in the geography category two fields focus on the increasingly vital resource of water total renewable water resources and freshwater withdrawal <\s>
<s> in the economy category three fields added for stock of direct foreign investment at home stock of direct foreign investment abroad and market value of publicly traded shares <\s>
<s> concise descriptions of all major religions included in the definitions and notes <\s>
<s> responsibility for printing of the world factbook turned over to the government printing office <\s>
<s> 2009 the online factbook site completely redesigned with many new features <\s>
<s> in the people category two new fields provide information on education in terms of opportunity and resources school life expectancy and education expenditures <\s>
<s> additionally the urbanization entry expanded to include all countries <\s>
<s> in the economy category five fields added central bank discount rate commercial bank prime lending rate stock of money stock of quasi money and stock of domestic credit <\s>
<s> 2010 in order to facilitate comparisons over time dozens of the entries in the economy category expanded to include two and in some cases three years worth of data <\s>
<s> a variety of enhancements introduced on the factbook web site <\s>
<s> 2011 weekly updates inaugurated on the the world factbook web site <\s>
<s> the dissolution of the netherlands antilles results in two new listings curacao and sint maarten <\s>
<s> a broadcast media field replaces the former radio broadcast stations and tv broadcast stations entries <\s>
<s> concise descriptions of all major legal systems incorporated into the definitions and notes <\s>
<s> in the geography section under natural hazards a volcanism subfield added for countries with historically active volcanoes <\s>
<s> in the government category a new national anthems field introduced <\s>
<s> about :: copyright and contributors the world factbook is prepared by the central intelligence agency for the use of us government officials and the style format coverage and content are designed to meet their specific requirements <\s>
<s> information is provided by antarctic information program national science foundation armed forces medical intelligence center department of defense bureau of the census department of commerce bureau of labor statistics department of labor central intelligence agency council of managers of national antarctic programs defense intelligence agency department of defense department of energy department of state fish and wildlife service department of the interior maritime administration department of transportation national geospatial-intelligence agency department of defense naval facilities engineering command department of defense office of insular affairs department of the interior office of naval intelligence department of defense us board on geographic names department of the interior us transportation command department of defense oil gas journal and other public and private sources <\s>
<s> the factbook is in the public domain <\s>
<s> accordingly it may be copied freely without permission of the central intelligence agency cia <\s>
<s> the official seal of the cia however may not be copied without permission as required by the cia act of 1949 50 u s c <\s>
<s> misuse of the official seal of the cia could result in civil and criminal penalties <\s>
<s> 1981 publication becomes an annual product and is renamed the world factbook <\s>
<s> a total of 165 nations are covered on 225 pages <\s>
<s> 1983 appendices conversion factors international organizations first introduced <\s>
<s> 1984 appendices expanded now include a <\s>
<s> the united nations b <\s>
<s> selected united nations organizations c <\s>
<s> selected international organizations d <\s>
<s> country membership in selected organizations e <\s>

<s> communications category split railroads highways inland waterways pipelines merchant marine and airports entries now make up a new transportation category <\s>
<s> the world factbook is first produced on cd-rom <\s>
<s> 1996 maps accompanying each entry now present more detail <\s>
<s> flags also introduced for nearly all entities <\s>
<s> various new entries appear under geography and communications <\s>
<s> factbook abbreviations consolidated into a new appendix a <\s>
<s> two new appendices present a cross-reference list of country data codes and a cross-reference list of hydrogeographic data codes <\s>
<s> geographic coordinates added to appendix h cross-reference list of geographic names <\s>
<s> factbook size expands by 95 pages in one year to reach 652 <\s>
<s> 1997 the world factbook introduced onto the internet <\s>
<s> a special printed edition prepared for the cia's 50th anniversary <\s>
<s> a schema or guide to country profiles introduced <\s>
<s> new color maps and flags now accompany each country profile <\s>
<s> category headings distinguished by shaded backgrounds <\s>
<s> number of categories expanded to nine the current number with the addition of an introduction for only a few countries and transnational issues which includes disputes-international and illicit drugs <\s>
<s> 1998 the introduction category with two entries current issues and historical perspective expanded to more countries <\s>
<s> last year for the production of cd-rom versions of the factbook <\s>
<s> 1999 historical perspective and current issues entries in the introduction category combined into a new background statement <\s>
<s> several new economy entries introduced <\s>
<s> a new physical map of the world added to the back-of-the-book reference maps <\s>
<s> 2000 a new country profile added on the southern ocean <\s>
<s> the background statements dramatically expanded to over 200 countries and possessions <\s>
<s> a number of new communications entries added <\s>
<s> 2001 background entries completed for all 267 entities in the factbook <\s>
<s> several new hiv aids entries introduced under the people category <\s>
<s> revision begun on individual country maps to include elevation extremes and a partial geographic grid <\s>
<s> weights and measures appendix deleted <\s>
<s> 2002 new entry on distribution of family income gini index added <\s>
<s> revision of individual country maps continued process still ongoing <\s>
<s> 2003 in the economy category petroleum entries added for oil production consumption exports imports and proved reserves as well as natural gas proved reserves <\s>
<s> 2004 bi-weekly updates launched on the world factbook web site <\s>
<s> additional petroleum entries included for natural gas production consumption exports and imports <\s>
<s> in the transportation category under merchant marine subfields added for foreign-owned vessels and those registered in other countries <\s>
<s> descriptions of the many forms of government mentioned in the factbook incorporated into the definitions and notes <\s>
<s> 2005 in the people category a major infectious diseases field added for countries deemed to pose a higher risk for travelers <\s>
<s> in the economy category entries included for current account balance investment public debt and reserves of foreign exchange and gold <\s>
<s> the transnational issues category expanded to include refugees and internally displaced persons <\s>
<s> category headings receive distinctive colored backgrounds <\s>
<s> these distinguishing colors are used in both the printed and online versions of the factbook <\s>
<s> size of the printed factbook reaches 702 pages <\s>
<s> 2006 in the economy category national gdp figures now presented at official exchange rates oer in addition to gdp at purchasing power parity ppp <\s>
<s> entries in the transportation section reordered highways changed to roadways and ports and harbors to ports and terminals <\s>
<s> 2007 in the government category the capital entry significantly expanded with up to four subfields including new information having to do with time <\s>
<s> the subfields consist of the name of the capital itself its geographic coordinates the time difference at the capital from coordinated universal time utc and if applicable information on daylight saving time dst <\s>
<s> where appropriate a special note is added to highlight those countries with multiple time zones <\s>
<s> a trafficking in persons entry added to the transnational issues category <\s>
<s> a new appendix weights and measures re introduced to the online version of the factbook <\s>
<s> 2008 in the geography category two fields focus on the increasingly vital resource of water total renewable water resources and freshwater withdrawal <\s>
<s> in the economy category three fields added for stock of direct foreign investment at home stock of direct foreign investment abroad and market value of publicly traded shares <\s>
<s> concise descriptions of all major religions included in the definitions and notes <\s>
<s> responsibility for printing of the world factbook turned over to the government printing office <\s>
<s> 2009 the online factbook site completely redesigned with many new features <\s>
<s> in the people category two new fields provide information on education in terms of opportunity and resources school life expectancy and education expenditures <\s>
<s> additionally the urbanization entry expanded to include all countries <\s>
<s> in the economy category five fields added central bank discount rate commercial bank prime lending rate stock of money stock of quasi money and stock of domestic credit <\s>
<s> 2010 in order to facilitate comparisons over time dozens of the entries in the economy category expanded to include two and in some cases three years worth of data <\s>
<s> a variety of enhancements introduced on the factbook web site <\s>
<s> 2011 weekly updates inaugurated on the the world factbook web site <\s>
<s> the dissolution of the netherlands antilles results in two new listings curacao and sint maarten <\s>
<s> a broadcast media field replaces the former radio broadcast stations and tv broadcast stations entries <\s>
<s> concise descriptions of all major legal systems incorporated into the definitions and notes <\s>
<s> in the geography section under natural hazards a volcanism subfield added for countries with historically active volcanoes <\s>
<s> in the government category a new national anthems field introduced <\s>
<s> about :: copyright and contributors the world factbook is prepared by the central intelligence agency for the use of us government officials and the style format coverage and content are designed to meet their specific requirements <\s>
<s> information is provided by antarctic information program national science foundation armed forces medical intelligence center department of defense bureau of the census department of commerce bureau of labor statistics department of labor central intelligence agency council of managers of national antarctic programs defense intelligence agency department of defense department of energy department of state fish and wildlife service department of the interior maritime administration department of transportation national geospatial-intelligence agency department of defense naval facilities engineering command department of defense office of insular affairs department of the interior office of naval intelligence department of defense us board on geographic names department of the interior us transportation command department of defense oil gas journal and other public and private sources <\s>
<s> the factbook is in the public domain <\s>
<s> accordingly it may be copied freely without permission of the central intelligence agency cia <\s>
<s> the official seal of the cia however may not be copied without permission as required by the cia act of 1949 50 u s c <\s>
<s> misuse of the official seal of the cia could result in civil and criminal penalties <\s>
<s> 1981 publication becomes an annual product and is renamed the world factbook <\s>
<s> a total of 165 nations are covered on 225 pages <\s>
<s> 1983 appendices conversion factors international organizations first introduced <\s>
<s> 1984 appendices expanded now include a <\s>
<s> the united nations b <\s>
<s> selected united nations organizations c <\s>
<s> selected international organizations d <\s>
<s> country membership in selected organizations e <\s>
<s> 1987 a new geography section replaces the former separate land and water sections <\s>
<s> un organizations and selected international organizations appendices merged into a new international organizations appendix <\s>
<s> 1988 more than 40 new geographic entities added to provide complete world coverage without overlap or omission <\s>
<s> among the new entities are antarctica oceans arctic atlantic indian pacific and the world <\s>
<s> the front-of-the-book explanatory introduction expanded and retitled to notes definitions and abbreviations <\s>
<s> two new appendices added weights and measures in place of conversion factors and a cross-reference list of geographic names <\s>
<s> factbook size reaches 300 pages <\s>
<s> 1989 economy section completely revised and now includes an overview briefly describing a country's economy <\s>
<s> new entries added under people government and communications <\s>
<s> 1990 the government section revised and considerably expanded with new entries <\s>
<s> 1991 a new international organizations and groups appendix added <\s>
<s> factbook size reaches 405 pages <\s>
<s> 1992 twenty new successor state entries replace those of the soviet union and yugoslavia <\s>
<s> new countries are respectively armenia azerbaijan belarus estonia georgia kazakhstan kyrgyzstan latvia lithuania moldova russia tajikistan turkmenistan ukraine uzbekistan and bosnia and hercegovina croatia macedonia serbia and montenegro slovenia <\s>
<s> number of nations in the factbook rises to 188 <\s>
<s> 1993 czechoslovakia's split necessitates new czech republic and slovakia entries <\s>
<s> new eritrea entry added after it secedes from ethiopia <\s>
<s> substantial enhancements made to geography section <\s>
<s> 1994 two new appendices address selected international environmental agreements <\s>
<s> the gross domestic product gdp of most developing countries changed to a purchasing power parity ppp basis rather than an exchange rate basis <\s>
<s> factbook size up to 512 pages <\s>

<s> several new hiv aids entries introduced under the people category <\s>
<s> revision begun on individual country maps to include elevation extremes and a partial geographic grid <\s>
<s> weights and measures appendix deleted <\s>
<s> 2002 new entry on distribution of family income gini index added <\s>
<s> revision of individual country maps continued process still ongoing <\s>
<s> 2003 in the economy category petroleum entries added for oil production consumption exports imports and proved reserves as well as natural gas proved reserves <\s>
<s> 2004 bi-weekly updates launched on the world factbook web site <\s>
<s> additional petroleum entries included for natural gas production consumption exports and imports <\s>
<s> in the transportation category under merchant marine subfields added for foreign-owned vessels and those registered in other countries <\s>
<s> descriptions of the many forms of government mentioned in the factbook incorporated into the definitions and notes <\s>
<s> 2005 in the people category a major infectious diseases field added for countries deemed to pose a higher risk for travelers <\s>
<s> in the economy category entries included for current account balance investment public debt and reserves of foreign exchange and gold <\s>
<s> the transnational issues category expanded to include refugees and internally displaced persons <\s>
<s> category headings receive distinctive colored backgrounds <\s>
<s> these distinguishing colors are used in both the printed and online versions of the factbook <\s>
<s> size of the printed factbook reaches 702 pages <\s>
<s> 2006 in the economy category national gdp figures now presented at official exchange rates oer in addition to gdp at purchasing power parity ppp <\s>
<s> entries in the transportation section reordered highways changed to roadways and ports and harbors to ports and terminals <\s>
<s> 2007 in the government category the capital entry significantly expanded with up to four subfields including new information having to do with time <\s>
<s> the subfields consist of the name of the capital itself its geographic coordinates the time difference at the capital from coordinated universal time utc and if applicable information on daylight saving time dst <\s>
<s> where appropriate a special note is added to highlight those countries with multiple time zones <\s>
<s> a trafficking in persons entry added to the transnational issues category <\s>
<s> a new appendix weights and measures re introduced to the online version of the factbook <\s>
<s> 2008 in the geography category two fields focus on the increasingly vital resource of water total renewable water resources and freshwater withdrawal <\s>
<s> in the economy category three fields added for stock of direct foreign investment at home stock of direct foreign investment abroad and market value of publicly traded shares <\s>
<s> concise descriptions of all major religions included in the definitions and notes <\s>
<s> responsibility for printing of the world factbook turned over to the government printing office <\s>
<s> 2009 the online factbook site completely redesigned with many new features <\s>
<s> in the people category two new fields provide information on education in terms of opportunity and resources school life expectancy and education expenditures <\s>
<s> additionally the urbanization entry expanded to include all countries <\s>
<s> in the economy category five fields added central bank discount rate commercial bank prime lending rate stock of money stock of quasi money and stock of domestic credit <\s>
<s> 2010 in order to facilitate comparisons over time dozens of the entries in the economy category expanded to include two and in some cases three years worth of data <\s>
<s> a variety of enhancements introduced on the factbook web site <\s>
<s> 2011 weekly updates inaugurated on the the world factbook web site <\s>
<s> the dissolution of the netherlands antilles results in two new listings curacao and sint maarten <\s>
<s> a broadcast media field replaces the former radio broadcast stations and tv broadcast stations entries <\s>
<s> concise descriptions of all major legal systems incorporated into the definitions and notes <\s>
<s> in the geography section under natural hazards a volcanism subfield added for countries with historically active volcanoes <\s>
<s> in the government category a new national anthems field introduced <\s>
<s> about :: copyright and contributors the world factbook is prepared by the central intelligence agency for the use of us government officials and the style format coverage and content are designed to meet their specific requirements <\s>
<s> information is provided by antarctic information program national science foundation armed forces medical intelligence center department of defense bureau of the census department of commerce bureau of labor statistics department of labor central intelligence agency council of managers of national antarctic programs defense intelligence agency department of defense department of energy department of state fish and wildlife service department of the interior maritime administration department of transportation national geospatial-intelligence agency department of defense naval facilities engineering command department of defense office of insular affairs department of the interior office of naval intelligence department of defense us board on geographic names department of the interior us transportation command department of defense oil gas journal and other public and private sources <\s>
<s> the factbook is in the public domain <\s>
<s> accordingly it may be copied freely without permission of the central intelligence agency cia <\s>
<s> the official seal of the cia however may not be copied without permission as required by the cia act of 1949 50 u s c <\s>
<s> misuse of the official seal of the cia could result in civil and criminal penalties <\s>
<s> 1981 publication becomes an annual product and is renamed the world factbook <\s>
<s> a total of 165 nations are covered on 225 pages <\s>
<s> 1983 appendices conversion factors international organizations first introduced <\s>
<s> 1984 appendices expanded now include a <\s>
<s> the united nations b <\s>
<s> selected united nations organizations c <\s>
<s> selected international organizations d <\s>
<s> country membership in selected organizations e <\s>
<s> 1987 a new geography section replaces the former separate land and water sections <\s>
<s> un organizations and selected international organizations appendices merged into a new international organizations appendix <\s>
<s> 1988 more than 40 new geographic entities added to provide complete world coverage without overlap or omission <\s>
<s> among the new entities are antarctica oceans arctic atlantic indian pacific and the world <\s>
<s> the front-of-the-book explanatory introduction expanded and retitled to notes definitions and abbreviations <\s>
<s> two new appendices added weights and measures in place of conversion factors and a cross-reference list of geographic names <\s>
<s> factbook size reaches 300 pages <\s>
<s> 1989 economy section completely revised and now includes an overview briefly describing a country's economy <\s>
<s> new entries added under people government and communications <\s>
<s> 1990 the government section revised and considerably expanded with new entries <\s>
<s> 1991 a new international organizations and groups appendix added <\s>
<s> factbook size reaches 405 pages <\s>
<s> 1992 twenty new successor state entries replace those of the soviet union and yugoslavia <\s>
<s> new countries are respectively armenia azerbaijan belarus estonia georgia kazakhstan kyrgyzstan latvia lithuania moldova russia tajikistan turkmenistan ukraine uzbekistan and bosnia and hercegovina croatia macedonia serbia and montenegro slovenia <\s>
<s> number of nations in the factbook rises to 188 <\s>
<s> 1993 czechoslovakia's split necessitates new czech republic and slovakia entries <\s>
<s> new eritrea entry added after it secedes from ethiopia <\s>
<s> substantial enhancements made to geography section <\s>
<s> 1994 two new appendices address selected international environmental agreements <\s>
<s> the gross domestic product gdp of most developing countries changed to a purchasing power parity ppp basis rather than an exchange rate basis <\s>
<s> factbook size up to 512 pages <\s>
<s> 1995 the gdp of all countries now presented on a ppp basis <\s>
<s> new appendix lists estimates of gdp on an exchange rate basis <\s>
<s> communications category split railroads highways inland waterways pipelines merchant marine and airports entries now make up a new transportation category <\s>
<s> the world factbook is first produced on cd-rom <\s>
<s> 1996 maps accompanying each entry now present more detail <\s>
<s> flags also introduced for nearly all entities <\s>
<s> various new entries appear under geography and communications <\s>
<s> factbook abbreviations consolidated into a new appendix a <\s>
<s> two new appendices present a cross-reference list of country data codes and a cross-reference list of hydrogeographic data codes <\s>
<s> geographic coordinates added to appendix h cross-reference list of geographic names <\s>
<s> factbook size expands by 95 pages in one year to reach 652 <\s>
<s> 1997 the world factbook introduced onto the internet <\s>
<s> a special printed edition prepared for the cia's 50th anniversary <\s>
<s> a schema or guide to country profiles introduced <\s>
<s> new color maps and flags now accompany each country profile <\s>
<s> category headings distinguished by shaded backgrounds <\s>
<s> number of categories expanded to nine the current number with the addition of an introduction for only a few countries and transnational issues which includes disputes-international and illicit drugs <\s>
<s> 1998 the introduction category with two entries current issues and historical perspective expanded to more countries <\s>
<s> last year for the production of cd-rom versions of the factbook <\s>
<s> 1999 historical perspective and current issues entries in the introduction category combined into a new background statement <\s>
<s> several new economy entries introduced <\s>
<s> a new physical map of the world added to the back-of-the-book reference maps <\s>
<s> 2000 a new country profile added on the southern ocean <\s>
<s> the background statements dramatically expanded to over 200 countries and possessions <\s>

<s> a trafficking in persons entry added to the transnational issues category <\s>
<s> a new appendix weights and measures re introduced to the online version of the factbook <\s>
<s> 2008 in the geography category two fields focus on the increasingly vital resource of water total renewable water resources and freshwater withdrawal <\s>
<s> in the economy category three fields added for stock of direct foreign investment at home stock of direct foreign investment abroad and market value of publicly traded shares <\s>
<s> concise descriptions of all major religions included in the definitions and notes <\s>
<s> responsibility for printing of the world factbook turned over to the government printing office <\s>
<s> 2009 the online factbook site completely redesigned with many new features <\s>
<s> in the people category two new fields provide information on education in terms of opportunity and resources school life expectancy and education expenditures <\s>
<s> additionally the urbanization entry expanded to include all countries <\s>
<s> in the economy category five fields added central bank discount rate commercial bank prime lending rate stock of money stock of quasi money and stock of domestic credit <\s>
<s> 2010 in order to facilitate comparisons over time dozens of the entries in the economy category expanded to include two and in some cases three years worth of data <\s>
<s> a variety of enhancements introduced on the factbook web site <\s>
<s> 2011 weekly updates inaugurated on the the world factbook web site <\s>
<s> the dissolution of the netherlands antilles results in two new listings curacao and sint maarten <\s>
<s> a broadcast media field replaces the former radio broadcast stations and tv broadcast stations entries <\s>
<s> concise descriptions of all major legal systems incorporated into the definitions and notes <\s>
<s> in the geography section under natural hazards a volcanism subfield added for countries with historically active volcanoes <\s>
<s> in the government category a new national anthems field introduced <\s>
<s> about :: copyright and contributors the world factbook is prepared by the central intelligence agency for the use of us government officials and the style format coverage and content are designed to meet their specific requirements <\s>
<s> information is provided by antarctic information program national science foundation armed forces medical intelligence center department of defense bureau of the census department of commerce bureau of labor statistics department of labor central intelligence agency council of managers of national antarctic programs defense intelligence agency department of defense department of energy department of state fish and wildlife service department of the interior maritime administration department of transportation national geospatial-intelligence agency department of defense naval facilities engineering command department of defense office of insular affairs department of the interior office of naval intelligence department of defense us board on geographic names department of the interior us transportation command department of defense oil gas journal and other public and private sources <\s>
<s> the factbook is in the public domain <\s>
<s> accordingly it may be copied freely without permission of the central intelligence agency cia <\s>
<s> the official seal of the cia however may not be copied without permission as required by the cia act of 1949 50 u s c <\s>
<s> misuse of the official seal of the cia could result in civil and criminal penalties <\s>
<s> 1981 publication becomes an annual product and is renamed the world factbook <\s>
<s> a total of 165 nations are covered on 225 pages <\s>
<s> 1983 appendices conversion factors international organizations first introduced <\s>
<s> 1984 appendices expanded now include a <\s>
<s> the united nations b <\s>
<s> selected united nations organizations c <\s>
<s> selected international organizations d <\s>
<s> country membership in selected organizations e <\s>
<s> 1987 a new geography section replaces the former separate land and water sections <\s>
<s> un organizations and selected international organizations appendices merged into a new international organizations appendix <\s>
<s> 1988 more than 40 new geographic entities added to provide complete world coverage without overlap or omission <\s>
<s> among the new entities are antarctica oceans arctic atlantic indian pacific and the world <\s>
<s> the front-of-the-book explanatory introduction expanded and retitled to notes definitions and abbreviations <\s>
<s> two new appendices added weights and measures in place of conversion factors and a cross-reference list of geographic names <\s>
<s> factbook size reaches 300 pages <\s>
<s> 1989 economy section completely revised and now includes an overview briefly describing a country's economy <\s>
<s> new entries added under people government and communications <\s>
<s> 1990 the government section revised and considerably expanded with new entries <\s>
<s> 1991 a new international organizations and groups appendix added <\s>
<s> factbook size reaches 405 pages <\s>
<s> 1992 twenty new successor state entries replace those of the soviet union and yugoslavia <\s>
<s> new countries are respectively armenia azerbaijan belarus estonia georgia kazakhstan kyrgyzstan latvia lithuania moldova russia tajikistan turkmenistan ukraine uzbekistan and bosnia and hercegovina croatia macedonia serbia and montenegro slovenia <\s>
<s> number of nations in the factbook rises to 188 <\s>
<s> 1993 czechoslovakia's split necessitates new czech republic and slovakia entries <\s>
<s> new eritrea entry added after it secedes from ethiopia <\s>
<s> substantial enhancements made to geography section <\s>
<s> 1994 two new appendices address selected international environmental agreements <\s>
<s> the gross domestic product gdp of most developing countries changed to a purchasing power parity ppp basis rather than an exchange rate basis <\s>
<s> factbook size up to 512 pages <\s>
<s> 1995 the gdp of all countries now presented on a ppp basis <\s>
<s> new appendix lists estimates of gdp on an exchange rate basis <\s>
<s> communications category split railroads highways inland waterways pipelines merchant marine and airports entries now make up a new transportation category <\s>
<s> the world factbook is first produced on cd-rom <\s>
<s> 1996 maps accompanying each entry now present more detail <\s>
<s> flags also introduced for nearly all entities <\s>
<s> various new entries appear under geography and communications <\s>
<s> factbook abbreviations consolidated into a new appendix a <\s>
<s> two new appendices present a cross-reference list of country data codes and a cross-reference list of hydrogeographic data codes <\s>
<s> geographic coordinates added to appendix h cross-reference list of geographic names <\s>
<s> factbook size expands by 95 pages in one year to reach 652 <\s>
<s> 1997 the world factbook introduced onto the internet <\s>
<s> a special printed edition prepared for the cia's 50th anniversary <\s>
<s> a schema or guide to country profiles introduced <\s>
<s> new color maps and flags now accompany each country profile <\s>
<s> category headings distinguished by shaded backgrounds <\s>
<s> number of categories expanded to nine the current number with the addition of an introduction for only a few countries and transnational issues which includes disputes-international and illicit drugs <\s>
<s> 1998 the introduction category with two entries current issues and historical perspective expanded to more countries <\s>
<s> last year for the production of cd-rom versions of the factbook <\s>
<s> 1999 historical perspective and current issues entries in the introduction category combined into a new background statement <\s>
<s> several new economy entries introduced <\s>
<s> a new physical map of the world added to the back-of-the-book reference maps <\s>
<s> 2000 a new country profile added on the southern ocean <\s>
<s> the background statements dramatically expanded to over 200 countries and possessions <\s>
<s> a number of new communications entries added <\s>
<s> 2001 background entries completed for all 267 entities in the factbook <\s>
<s> several new hiv aids entries introduced under the people category <\s>
<s> revision begun on individual country maps to include elevation extremes and a partial geographic grid <\s>
<s> weights and measures appendix deleted <\s>
<s> 2002 new entry on distribution of family income gini index added <\s>
<s> revision of individual country maps continued process still ongoing <\s>
<s> 2003 in the economy category petroleum entries added for oil production consumption exports imports and proved reserves as well as natural gas proved reserves <\s>
<s> 2004 bi-weekly updates launched on the world factbook web site <\s>
<s> additional petroleum entries included for natural gas production consumption exports and imports <\s>
<s> in the transportation category under merchant marine subfields added for foreign-owned vessels and those registered in other countries <\s>
<s> descriptions of the many forms of government mentioned in the factbook incorporated into the definitions and notes <\s>
<s> 2005 in the people category a major infectious diseases field added for countries deemed to pose a higher risk for travelers <\s>
<s> in the economy category entries included for current account balance investment public debt and reserves of foreign exchange and gold <\s>
<s> the transnational issues category expanded to include refugees and internally displaced persons <\s>
<s> category headings receive distinctive colored backgrounds <\s>
<s> these distinguishing colors are used in both the printed and online versions of the factbook <\s>
<s> size of the printed factbook reaches 702 pages <\s>
<s> 2006 in the economy category national gdp figures now presented at official exchange rates oer in addition to gdp at purchasing power parity ppp <\s>
<s> entries in the transportation section reordered highways changed to roadways and ports and harbors to ports and terminals <\s>
<s> 2007 in the government category the capital entry significantly expanded with up to four subfields including new information having to do with time <\s>
<s> the subfields consist of the name of the capital itself its geographic coordinates the time difference at the capital from coordinated universal time utc and if applicable information on daylight saving time dst <\s>
<s> where appropriate a special note is added to highlight those countries with multiple time zones <\s>
<s> a trafficking in persons entry added to the transnational issues category <\s>
<s> a new appendix weights and measures re introduced to the online version of the factbook <\s>
